All domestic transactions like funds transfers, online, swiping machines, UPI and ATM withdrawals will continue to work seamlessly.

Best,
Team Niyo

12/04/2023, 09:39 - Dhruval Bhuva: Dear Dhruval,

 

Thank you for your message.

Withdrawal from a course is only possible within 14 days after registration.

Unfortunately, it is no longer possible to cancel your language course due to our terms and conditions!

Here is an excerpt from our terms and conditions:

“Revocation/Cancellation by the participant

Registration for a training/course may be revoked within 14 days after registration without giving any reasons. Revocation must be made in writing to the Campus for Professional Development and Language Proficiency.

Cancellation is free of charge if it is made until three weeks before the first session. After this, or in case of non-attendance, the full fee will be due. The date the cancellation is received is decisive. After previous agreement with us, you can of course name a replacement candidate.”

https://www.thws.de/en/further-education-thws/wer-wir-sind/terms-and-conditions-for-campus-for-professional-development-and-campus-for-language-proficiency/

 

If you are unable to attend the course but the cancellation period has passed, we recommend the following:

Try to take part in the course as much as possible.    
Complete the exercises posted on the e-learning platform (THWS Moodle platform) autonomously.
Work through the textbook by yourself.
Take the final exam at the end of the course, even if you did not take the course.
Note: You must register for the exam before you can take it. If you don't pass the exam the first time, you can retake it for free within one year.
 

By following our recommendations, the required course fee is not wasted.

 

Best regards,

Campus Sprache

#include <sensor.h>

// Define the callback function to handle sensor events
static void sensor_callback(sensor_h sensor, sensor_event_s *event, void *user_data) {
    // Check if the sensor is the accelerometer
    if (sensor_get_type(sensor) == SENSOR_ACCELEROMETER) {
        // Retrieve the raw sensor data from the event structure
        float x = event->values[0];
        float y = event->values[1];
        float z = event->values[2];
        
        // Process the raw sensor data as needed
        // ...
        
        // Print the raw sensor data
        printf("Raw Accelerometer Data: X=%.2f, Y=%.2f, Z=%.2f\n", x, y, z);
    }
}

// Main function
int main(int argc, char *argv[]) {
    // Initialize the sensor
    sensor_h accelerometer;
    sensor_get_default_sensor(SENSOR_ACCELEROMETER, &accelerometer);
    
    // Register the sensor event callback
    sensor_listener_h listener;
    sensor_create_listener(accelerometer, &listener);
    sensor_listener_set_event_cb(listener, 100, sensor_callback, NULL);
    
    // Start the sensor listener
    sensor_listener_start(listener);
    
    // Run the main loop or perform other tasks
    
    // Stop the sensor listener when you're done
    sensor_listener_stop(listener);
    sensor_destroy_listener(listener);
    
    return 0;
}
